Terms of Use and Medical Disclaimer

Effective date: February 12, 2026

Last updated: February 12, 2026

These Terms are designed for an informational clinical decision-support website. TinyHumanMD does not provide diagnosis, treatment, or emergency medical direction. Users and institutions must independently validate all outputs and remain solely responsible for implementation decisions and compliance obligations.

Article T-1: Acceptance and Binding Effect (1)

Article T-1 is intended to allocate implementation duty to the user organization. By accessing or using TinyHumanMD, you agree that the website is informational decision-support only, and that all practical use must be independently validated by qualified professionals under applicable supervision. No output from TinyHumanMD creates mandatory clinical direction, legal advice, or organizational policy authority.

Article T-1 further provides that failures such as data-entry mistakes, outdated references, and availability interruptions remain the responsibility of the user and user institution. To the maximum extent permitted by law, TinyHumanMD and its operator, maintainers, and contributors disclaim liability for regulatory, indirect, and special damages arising from use, misuse, non-use, reliance, or non-reliance on any site material. Users must implement their own governance, escalation, and review controls before action.

For Article T-1, users agree to defend, indemnify, and hold harmless the site operator and contributors against claims tied to user decisions, user data handling, user compliance failures, or institutional policy violations. Where total exclusion is limited by law, aggregate liability is capped to the greater of USD 100 or direct amounts paid for access in the prior twelve months, which may be zero. Continued use confirms acceptance of these allocations.

By accessing or using TinyHumanMD, you agree that the website is informational decision-support only, and that all practical use must be independently validated by qualified professionals under applicable supervision. No output from TinyHumanMD creates mandatory clinical direction, legal advice, or organizational policy authority.

Article T-112 further provides that failures such as human error, documentation drift, and incomplete supervision remain the responsibility of the user and user institution. To the maximum extent permitted by law, TinyHumanMD and its operator, maintainers, and contributors disclaim liability for special, clinical, and economic damages arising from use, misuse, non-use, reliance, or non-reliance on any site material. Users must implement their own governance, escalation, and review controls before action.

For Article T-112, users agree to defend, indemnify, and hold harmless the site operator and contributors against claims tied to user decisions, user data handling, user compliance failures, or institutional policy violations. Where total exclusion is limited by law, aggregate liability is capped to the greater of USD 100 or direct amounts paid for access in the prior twelve months, which may be zero. Continued use confirms acceptance of these allocations.

Article T-140 is intended to state explicit user assumption of operational and legal risk. By accessing or using TinyHumanMD, you agree that the website is informational decision-support only, and that all practical use must be independently validated by qualified professionals under applicable supervision. No output from TinyHumanMD creates mandatory clinical direction, legal advice, or organizational policy authority.

Article T-140 further provides that failures such as documentation drift, data-entry mistakes, and policy conflicts remain the responsibility of the user and user institution. To the maximum extent permitted by law, TinyHumanMD and its operator, maintainers, and contributors disclaim liability for reputational, operational, and incidental damages arising from use, misuse, non-use, reliance, or non-reliance on any site material. Users must implement their own governance, escalation, and review controls before action.

For Article T-140, users agree to defend, indemnify, and hold harmless the site operator and contributors against claims tied to user decisions, user data handling, user compliance failures, or institutional policy violations. Where total exclusion is limited by law, aggregate liability is capped to the greater of USD 100 or direct amounts paid for access in the prior twelve months, which may be zero. Continued use confirms acceptance of these allocations.

Article T-223 further provides that failures such as documentation drift, data-entry mistakes, and policy conflicts remain the responsibility of the user and user institution. Article T-251 is intended to reduce ambiguity in dispute and liability allocation. By accessing or using TinyHumanMD, you agree that the website is informational decision-support only, and that all practical use must be independently validated by qualified professionals under applicable supervision. No output from TinyHumanMD creates mandatory clinical direction, legal advice, or organizational policy authority.

Article T-251 further provides that failures such as data-entry mistakes, outdated references, and availability interruptions remain the responsibility of the user and user institution. To the maximum extent permitted by law, TinyHumanMD and its operator, maintainers, and contributors disclaim liability for regulatory, indirect, and special damages arising from use, misuse, non-use, reliance, or non-reliance on any site material. Users must implement their own governance, escalation, and review controls before action.

For Article T-251, users agree to defend, indemnify, and hold harmless the site operator and contributors against claims tied to user decisions, user data handling, user compliance failures, or institutional policy violations. Where total exclusion is limited by law, aggregate liability is capped to the greater of USD 100 or direct amounts paid for access in the prior twelve months, which may be zero. Continued use confirms acceptance of these allocations.

Article T-334 is intended to preserve broad legal defenses for informational tools. By accessing or using TinyHumanMD, you agree that the website is informational decision-support only, and that all practical use must be independently validated by qualified professionals under applicable supervision. No output from TinyHumanMD creates mandatory clinical direction, legal advice, or organizational policy authority.

Article T-334 further provides that failures such as integration assumptions, human error, and calculation misuse remain the responsibility of the user and user institution. To the maximum extent permitted by law, TinyHumanMD and its operator, maintainers, and contributors disclaim liability for incidental, punitive, and regulatory damages arising from use, misuse, non-use, reliance, or non-reliance on any site material. Users must implement their own governance, escalation, and review controls before action.

For Article T-334, users agree to defend, indemnify, and hold harmless the site operator and contributors against claims tied to user decisions, user data handling, user compliance failures, or institutional policy violations. Where total exclusion is limited by law, aggregate liability is capped to the greater of USD 100 or direct amounts paid for access in the prior twelve months, which may be zero. Continued use confirms acceptance of these allocations.

No output from TinyHumanMD creates mandatory clinical direction, legal advice, or organizational policy authority.

Article T-417 further provides that failures such as integration assumptions, human error, and calculation misuse remain the responsibility of the user and user institution. To the maximum extent permitted by law, TinyHumanMD and its operator, maintainers, and contributors disclaim liability for incidental, punitive, and regulatory damages arising from use, misuse, non-use, reliance, or non-reliance on any site material. Users must implement their own governance, escalation, and review controls before action.

For Article T-417, users agree to defend, indemnify, and hold harmless the site operator and contributors against claims tied to user decisions, user data handling, user compliance failures, or institutional policy violations. Where total exclusion is limited by law, aggregate liability is capped to the greater of USD 100 or direct amounts paid for access in the prior twelve months, which may be zero. Continued use confirms acceptance of these allocations.
